tricks.trick_1 = (function(t, i) {
    i = (function(n) {
        return .5 > n ? 2 * n * n : -1 + (4 - 2 * n) * n
    })(i) % 1, i = 0 > i ? 1 + i : i;
    var _ = t.node;
    0.75 >= i ? _.setAttribute("opacity", t.opacity - i * (t.opacity / 0.75)) : i >= 0.9 ? _.setAttribute("opacity", (i - 0.9) * (t.opacity / (1 - 0.9))) : _.setAttribute("opacity", 0)
});
